# Kubernetes Controller Runtime Reconciler Registration

## Your Task

Trace how a controller registers itself with the controller-runtime Manager in kubernetes/kubernetes. Find the Go source files that define the Reconciler interface, implement SetupWithManager, and wire the controller into the manager's reconcile loop.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the crossrepo tracing domain.

## Available Resources

The local `/workspace/` directory contains: sg-evals/kubernetes--v1.32.0, sg-evals/client-go--v0.32.0, sg-evals/api--v0.32.0, sg-evals/etcd-io-etcd.

**Note:** Additional repositories are accessible via Sourcegraph MCP tools:
- `sg-evals/etcd-io-etcd` (etcd-io/etcd)


    26→// EndpointReconciler knows how to reconcile the endpoints for the apiserver service.
    27→type EndpointReconciler interface {
    28→	// ReconcileEndpoints sets the endpoints for the given apiserver service (ro or rw).
    29→	// ReconcileEndpoints expects that the endpoints objects it manages will all be
    30→	// managed only by ReconcileEndpoints; therefore, to understand this, you need only
    31→	// understand the requirements.
    32→	//
    33→	// Requirements:
    34→	//  * All apiservers MUST use the same ports for their {rw, ro} services.
    35→	//  * All apiservers MUST use ReconcileEndpoints and only ReconcileEndpoints to manage the
    36→	//      endpoints for their {rw, ro} services.
    37→	//  * ReconcileEndpoints is called periodically from all apiservers.
    38→	ReconcileEndpoints(serviceName string, ip net.IP, endpointPorts []corev1.EndpointPort, reconcilePorts bool) error

    98→func newDeploymentControllerDescriptor() *ControllerDescriptor {
    99→	return &ControllerDescriptor{
   100→		name:     names.DeploymentController,
   101→		aliases:  []string{"deployment"},
   102→		initFunc: startDeploymentController,
   103→	}
   104→}
   105→
   106→func startDeploymentController(ctx context.Context, controllerContext ControllerContext, controllerName string) (controller.Interface, bool, error) {
   107→	dc, err := deployment.NewDeploymentController(
   108→		ctx,
   109→		controllerContext.InformerFactory.Apps().V1().Deployments(),
   110→		controllerContext.InformerFactory.Apps().V1().ReplicaSets(),
   111→		controllerContext.InformerFactory.Core().V1().Pods(),
   112→		controllerContext.ClientBuilder.ClientOrDie("deployment-controller"),
   113→	)
   114→	if err != nil {
   115→		return nil, true, fmt.Errorf("error creating Deployment controller: %v", err)
   116→	}
   117→	go dc.Run(ctx, int(controllerContext.ComponentConfig.DeploymentController.ConcurrentDeploymentSyncs))
   118→	return nil, true, nil
   119→}

118-assistanttext-
Perfect! I've created a comprehensive answer to trace how controllers register with the Kubernetes controller manager. Here's a summary of my findings:

## Key Discoveries

**Kubernetes uses its own native controller framework** rather than the controller-runtime library. The registration pattern works as follows:

### Core Components Found:

1. **Reconciler Pattern** (`DeploymentController` in `pkg/controller/deployment/deployment_controller.go`):
   - Struct-based approach with client, listers, work queue, and event recorder
   - Implements reconciliation through a `syncHandler` function

2. **Manager Equivalent** (`ControllerContext` in `cmd/kube-controller-manager/app/controllermanager.go`):
   - Provides InformerFactory, ClientBuilder, and ComponentConfig to controllers
   - Manages the overall control plane lifecycle

3. **SetupWithManager Equivalent** (Split into two parts):
   - **Initialization**: `NewDeploymentController()` registers informer event handlers
   - **Manager Integration**: `startDeploymentController()` instantiates and calls `Run()`

4. **Reconciliation Loop**:
   - `Run()` method spawns worker goroutines
   - Workers process items from the work queue continuously
   - Informer event handlers enqueue items when changes occur

### Registration Chain:
```
Run() → CreateControllerContext() → StartControllers() → 
startDeploymentController() → NewDeploymentController() → Run(ctx, workers)
```

The answer.json file includes file paths, key symbols, and a detailed narrative explaining how the Kubernetes controller registration pattern works—showing both the manager-level wiring and the individual controller implementations.

{\n\t\t\tdesiredEndpointsByPortMap[epHash].Insert(&endpoint)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tspMetrics := metrics.NewServicePortCache()\n\ttotalAdded := 0\n\ttotalRemoved := 0\n\n\t// Determine changes necessary for each group of slices by port map.\n\tfor portMap, desiredEndpoints := range desiredEndpointsByPortMap {\n\t\tnumEndpoints := len(desiredEndpoints)\n\t\tpmSlicesToCreate, pmSlicesToUpdate, of the core control flow\n\t\tplaceholderSlice := newEndpointSlice(logger, service, &endpointMeta{ports: []discovery.EndpointPort{}, addressType: addressType}, r.controllerName)\n\t\tif len(slicesToDelete) == 1 && placeholderSliceCompare.DeepEqual(slicesToDelete[0], placeholderSlice) {\n\t\t\t// We are about to unnecessarily delete/recreate the placeholder, remove it now.\n\t\t\tslicesToDelete = slicesToDelete[:0]\n\t\t} else {\n\t\t\tslicesToCreate = append(slicesToCreate, placeholderSlice)\n\t\t}\n\t\tspMetrics.Set(endpointsliceutil.NewPortMapKey(placeholderSlice.Ports), metrics.EfficiencyInfo{\n\t\t\tEndpoints: 0,\n\t\t\tSlices:    1,\n\t\t})\n\t}\n\n\tmetrics.EndpointsAddedPerSync.WithLabelValues().Observe(float64(totalAdded))\n\tmetrics.EndpointsRemovedPerSync.WithLabelValues().Observe(float64(totalRemoved))\n\n\tserviceNN := types.NamespacedName{Name: service.Name, Namespace: service.Namespace}\n\tr.metricsCache.UpdateServicePortCache(serviceNN, spMetrics)\n\n\t// Topology hints are assigned per address type. We need to do 2 things:\n\t\t//  1. If hints were added previously based on the annotation, we need to\n\t\t//     clear up any locally cached hints from the topologyCache object.\n\t\t//  2. Optionally remove the actual hints from the EndpointSlice if we know\n\t\t//     that the `trafficDistribution` field is also NOT being used. In other\n\t\t//     words, if we know that the `trafficDistribution` field has been\n\t\t//     correctly configured by the customer, we DO NOT remove the hints and\n\t\t//     wait for the trafficDist handlers to correctly configure them. Always\n\t\t//     unconditionally removing hints here (and letting them get readded by\n\t\t//     the trafficDist) adds extra overhead in the form of DeepCopy (done\n\t\t//     within topologyCache.RemoveHints)\n\n\t\t// Check 1.\n\t\tif r.topologyCache != nil {\n\t\t\tif r.topologyCache.HasPopulatedHints(si.ServiceKey) {\n\t\t\t\tlogger.Info(\"TopologyAwareHints annotation has changed, removing hints\", \"serviceKey\", si.ServiceKey, \"addressType\", si.AddressType)\n\t\t\t\tevents = append(events, &topologycache.EventBuilder{\n\t\t\t\t\tEventType: corev1.EventTypeWarning,\n\t\t\t\t\tReason:    \"TopologyAwareHintsDisabled\",\n\t\t\t\t\tMessage:   topologycache.FormatWithAddressType(topologycache.TopologyAwareHintsDisabled, si.AddressType),\n\t\t\t\t})\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tr.topologyCache.RemoveHints(si.ServiceKey, addressType)\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// Check 2.\n\t\tif !canUseTrafficDistribution {\n\t\t\tslicesToCreate, slicesToUpdate = topologycache.RemoveHintsFromSlices(si)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tif canUseTrafficDistribution {\n\t\tr.metricsCache.UpdateTrafficDistributionForService(serviceNN, service.Spec.TrafficDistribution)\n\t\tslicesToCreate, slicesToUpdate, _ = trafficdist.ReconcileHints(service.Spec.TrafficDistribution, slicesToCreate, slicesToUpdate, unchangedSlices(existingSlices, slicesToUpdate, slicesToDelete))\n\t} else {\n\t\tr.metricsCache.UpdateTrafficDistributionForService(serviceNN, nil)\n\t}\n\n\terr := r.finalize(service, slicesToCreate, slicesToUpdate, slicesToDelete, triggerTime)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\terrs = append(errs, err)\n\t}\n\tfor _, event := range events {\n\t\tr.eventRecorder.Event(service, event.EventType, event.Reason, event.Message)\n\t}\n\treturn utilerrors.NewAggregate(errs)\n\n}\n\nfunc NewReconciler(client clientset.Interface, nodeLister corelisters.NodeLister, maxEndpointsPerSlice int32, endpointSliceTracker *endpointsliceutil.EndpointSliceTracker, topologyCache *topologycache.TopologyCache, eventRecorder record.EventRecorder, controllerName string, options ...ReconcilerOption) *Reconciler {\n\tr := &Reconciler{\n\t\tclient:               client,\n\t\tnodeLister:           nodeLister,\n\t\tmaxEndpointsPerSlice: maxEndpointsPerSlice,\n\t\tendpointSliceTracker: endpointSliceTracker,\n\t\tmetricsCache:         metrics.NewCache(maxEndpointsPerSlice),\n\t\ttopologyCache:        topologyCache,\n\t\teventRecorder:        eventRecorder,\n\t\tcontrollerName:       controllerName,\n\t}\n\tfor _, option := range options {\n\t\toption(r)\n\t}\n\treturn r\n}\n\n// placeholderSliceCompare is a conversion func for comparing two placeholder endpoint slices.\n// It only compares the specific fields we care about.\nvar placeholderSliceCompare = conversion.EqualitiesOrDie(\n\tfunc(a, b metav1.OwnerReference) bool {\n\t\treturn a.String() == b.String()\n\t},\n\tfunc(a, b metav1.ObjectMeta) bool {\n\t\tif a.Namespace != b.Namespace {\n\t\t\treturn false\n\t\t}\n\t\tfor k, v := range a.Labels {\n\t\t\tif b.Labels[k] != v {\n\t\t\t\treturn false\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t\tfor k, v := range b.Labels {\n\t\t\tif a.Labels[k] != v {\n\t\t\t\treturn false\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t\treturn true\n\t},\n)\n\n// finalize creates, updates, and deletes slices as specified\nfunc (r *Reconciler) finalize(\n\tservice *corev1.Service,\n\tslicesToCreate,\n\tslicesToUpdate,\n\tslicesToDelete []*discovery.EndpointSlice,\n\ttriggerTime time.Time,\n) error {\n\t// If there are slices to create and delete, change the creates to updates\n\t// of the slices that would otherwise be deleted.\n\tfor i := 0; i < len(slicesToDelete); {\n\t\tif len(slicesToCreate) == 0 {\n\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t}\n\t\tsliceToDelete := slicesToDelete[i]\n\t\tslice := slicesToCreate[len(slicesToCreate)-1]\n\t\t// Only update EndpointSlices that are owned by this Service and have\n\t\t// the same AddressType. We need to avoid updating EndpointSlices that\n\t\t// are being garbage collected for an old Service with the same name.\n\t\t// The AddressType field is immutable. Since Services also consider\n\t\t// IPFamily immutable, the only case where this should matter will be\n\t\t// the migration from IP to IPv4 and IPv6 AddressTypes, where there's a\n\t\t// chance EndpointSlices with an IP AddressType would otherwise be\n\t\t// updated to IPv4 or IPv6 without this check.\n\t\tif sliceToDelete.AddressType == slice.AddressType && ownedBy(sliceToDelete, service) {\n\t\t\tslice.Name = sliceToDelete.Name\n\t\t\tslicesToCreate = slicesToCreate[:len(slicesToCreate)-1]\n\t\t\tslicesToUpdate = append(slicesToUpdate, slice)\n\t\t\tslicesToDelete = append(slicesToDelete[:i], slicesToDelete[i+1:]...)\n\t\t} else {\n\t\t\ti++\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// Don't create new EndpointSlices if the Service is pending deletion. This\n\t// is to avoid a potential race condition with the garbage collector where\n\t// it tries to delete EndpointSlices as this controller replaces them.\n\tif service.DeletionTimestamp == nil {\n\t\tfor _, endpointSlice := range slicesToCreate {\n\t\t\taddTriggerTimeAnnotation(endpointSlice, triggerTime)\n\t\t\tcreatedSlice, err := r.client.DiscoveryV1().EndpointSlices(service.Namespace).Create(context.TODO(), endpointSlice, metav1.CreateOptions{})\n\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\t// If the namespace is terminating, creates will continue to fail. Simply drop the item.\n\t\t\t\tif errors.HasStatusCause(err, corev1.NamespaceTerminatingCause) {\n\t\t\t\t\treturn nil\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"failed to create EndpointSlice for Service %s/%s: %v\", service.Namespace, service.Name, err)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tr.endpointSliceTracker.Update(createdSlice)\n\t\t\tmetrics.EndpointSliceChanges.WithLabelValues(\"create\").Inc()\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tfor _, endpointSlice := range slicesToUpdate {\n\t\taddTriggerTimeAnnotation(endpointSlice, triggerTime)\n\t\tupdatedSlice, err := r.client.DiscoveryV1().EndpointSlices(service.Namespace).Update(context.TODO(), endpointSlice, metav1.UpdateOptions{})\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"failed to update %s EndpointSlice for Service %s/%s: %v\", endpointSlice.Name, service.Namespace, service.Name, err)\n\t\t}\n\t\tr.endpointSliceTracker.Update(updatedSlice)\n\t\tmetrics.EndpointSliceChanges.WithLabelValues(\"update\").Inc()\n\t}\n\n\tfor _, endpointSlice := range slicesToDelete {\n\t\terr := r.client.DiscoveryV1().EndpointSlices(service.Namespace).Delete(context.TODO(), endpointSlice.Name, metav1.DeleteOptions{})\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"failed to delete %s service.Spec.TrafficDistribution != nil && *service.Spec.TrafficDistribution == corev1.ServiceTrafficDistributionPreferClose {\n\t\t\ttrafficDistribution = *service.Spec.TrafficDistribution\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tnumSlicesChanged := len(slicesToCreate) + len(slicesToUpdate) + len(slicesToDelete)\n\tmetrics.EndpointSlicesChangedPerSync.WithLabelValues(topologyLabel, trafficDistribution).Observe(float64(numSlicesChanged))\n\n\treturn nil\n}\n\n// reconcileByPortMapping compares the endpoints found in existing slices with\n// the list of desired endpoints and returns lists of slices to create, update,\n// and delete. It also checks that the slices mirror the parent services labels.\n// The logic is split up into several main steps:\n//  1. Iterate through existing slices, delete endpoints that are no longer\n//     desired and update matching endpoints that have changed. It also checks\n//     if the slices have the labels of the parent services, and updates them if not.\n//  2. Iterate through slices that have been modified in 1 and fill them up with\n//     any remaining desired endpoints.\n//  3. If there still desired endpoints left, try to fit them into a previously\n//     unchanged slice and/or create new ones.\nfunc (r *Reconciler) reconcileByPortMapping(\n\tlogger klog.Logger,\n\tservice *corev1.Service,\n\texistingSlices []*discovery.EndpointSlice,\n\tdesiredSet endpointsliceutil.EndpointSet,\n\tendpointMeta *endpointMeta,\n) ([]*discovery.EndpointSlice, []*discovery.EndpointSlice, []*discovery.EndpointSlice, int, int) {\n\tslicesByName := map[string]*discovery.EndpointSlice{}\n\tsliceNamesUnchanged := sets.New[string]()\n\tsliceNamesToUpdate := sets.New[string]()\n\tsliceNamesToDelete := sets.New[string]()\n\tnumRemoved := 0\n\n\t// 1. Iterate through existing slices to delete endpoints no longer desired\n\t//    and update endpoints that have changed\n\tfor _, existingSlice := range existingSlices {\n\t\tslicesByName[existingSlice.Name] = existingSlice\n\t\tnewEndpoints := []discovery.Endpoint{}\n\t\tendpointUpdated := false\n\t\tfor _, endpoint := range existingSlice.Endpoints {\n\t\t\tgot := desiredSet.Get(&endpoint)\n\t\t\t// If endpoint is desired add it to list of endpoints to keep.\n\t\t\tif got != nil {\n\t\t\t\tnewEndpoints = append(newEndpoints, *got)\n\t\t\t\t// If existing version of endpoint doesn't match desired version\n\t\t\t\t// set endpointUpdated to ensure endpoint changes are persisted.\n\t\t\t\tif !endpointsliceutil.EndpointsEqualBeyondHash(got, &endpoint) {\n\t\t\t\t\tendpointUpdated = true\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\t// once an endpoint has been placed/found in a slice, it no\n\t\t\t\t// longer needs to be handled\n\t\t\t\tdesiredSet.Delete(&endpoint)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// generate the slice labels and check if parent labels have changed\n\t\tlabels, labelsChanged := setEndpointSliceLabels(logger, existingSlice, service, r.controllerName)\n\n\t\t// If an endpoint was updated or removed, mark for update or delete\n\t\tif endpointUpdated || len(existingSlice.Endpoints) != len(newEndpoints) {\n\t\t\tif len(existingSlice.Endpoints) > len(newEndpoints) {\n\t\t\t\tnumRemoved += len(existingSlice.Endpoints) - len(newEndpoints)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tif len(newEndpoints) == 0 {\n\t\t\t\t// if no endpoints desired in this slice, mark for deletion\n\t\t\t\tsliceNamesToDelete.Insert(existingSlice.Name)\n\t\t\t} else {\n\t\t\t\t// otherwise, copy and mark for update\n\t\t\t\tepSlice := existingSlice.DeepCopy()\n\t\t\t\tepSlice.Endpoints = newEndpoints\n\t\t\t\tepSlice.Labels = labels\n\t\t\t\tslicesByName[existingSlice.Name] = epSlice\n\t\t\t\tsliceNamesToUpdate.Insert(epSlice.Name)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t} else if labelsChanged {\n\t\t\t// if labels have changed, copy and mark for update\n\t\t\tepSlice := existingSlice.DeepCopy()\n\t\t\tepSlice.Labels = labels\n\t\t\tslicesByName[existingSlice.Name] = epSlice\n\t\t\tsliceNamesToUpdate.Insert(epSlice.Name)\n\t\t} else {\n\t\t\t// slices with no changes will be useful if there are leftover endpoints\n\t\t\tsliceNamesUnchanged.Insert(existingSlice.Name)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tnumAdded := desiredSet.Len()\n\n\t// 2. If we still have desired endpoints to add and slices marked for update,\n\t//    iterate through the slices and fill them up with the desired endpoints.\n\tif desiredSet.Len() > 0 && sliceNamesToUpdate.Len() > 0 {\n\t\tslices := []*discovery.EndpointSlice{}\n\t\tfor _, sliceName := range sliceNamesToUpdate.UnsortedList() {\n\t\t\tslices = append(slices, slicesByName[sliceName])\n\t\t}\n\t\t// Sort endpoint slices by length so we're filling up the fullest ones\n\t\t// first.\n\t\tsort.Sort(endpointSliceEndpointLen(slices))\n\n\t\t// Iterate through slices and fill them up with desired endpoints.\n\t\tfor _, slice := range slices {\n\t\t\tfor desiredSet.Len() > 0 && len(slice.Endpoints) < int(r.maxEndpointsPerSlice) {\n\t\t\t\tendpoint, _ := desiredSet.PopAny()\n\t\t\t\tslice.Endpoints = append(slice.Endpoints, *endpoint)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// 3. If there are still desired endpoints left at this point, we try to fit\n\t//    the endpoints in a single existing slice. If there are no slices with\n\t//    that capacity, we create new slices for the endpoints.\n\tslicesToCreate := []*discovery.EndpointSlice{}\n\n\tfor desiredSet.Len() > 0 {\n\t\tvar sliceToFill *discovery.EndpointSlice\n\n\t\t// If the remaining amounts of endpoints is smaller than the max\n\t\t// endpoints per slice and we have slices that haven't already been\n\t\t// filled, try to fit them in one.\n\t\tif desiredSet.Len() < int(r.maxEndpointsPerSlice) && sliceNamesUnchanged.Len() > 0 {\n\t\t\tunchangedSlices := []*discovery.EndpointSlice{}\n\t\t\tfor _, sliceName := range sliceNamesUnchanged.UnsortedList() {\n\t\t\t\tunchangedSlices = append(unchangedSlices, slicesByName[sliceName])\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tsliceToFill = getSliceToFill(unchangedSlices, desiredSet.Len(), int(r.maxEndpointsPerSlice))\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// If we didn't find a sliceToFill, generate a new empty one.\n\t\tif sliceToFill == nil {\n\t\t\tsliceToFill = newEndpointSlice(logger, service, endpointMeta, r.controllerName)\n\t\t} else {\n\t\t\t// deep copy required to modify this slice.\n\t\t\tsliceToFill = sliceToFill.DeepCopy()\n\t\t\tslicesByName[sliceToFill.Name] = sliceToFill\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// Fill the slice up with remaining endpoints.\n\t\tfor desiredSet.Len() > 0 && len(sliceToFill.Endpoints) < int(r.maxEndpointsPerSlice) {\n\t\t\tendpoint, _ := desiredSet.PopAny()\n\t\t\tsliceToFill.Endpoints = append(sliceToFill.Endpoints, *endpoint)\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// New slices will not have a Name set, use this to determine whether\n\t\t// this should be append(slicesToCreate, sliceToFill)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// Build slicesToUpdate from slice names.\n\tslicesToUpdate := []*discovery.EndpointSlice{}\n\tfor _, sliceName := range sliceNamesToUpdate.UnsortedList() {\n\t\tslicesToUpdate = append(slicesToUpdate, slicesByName[sliceName])\n\t}\n\n\t// Build slicesToDelete from slice names.\n\tslicesToDelete := []*discovery.EndpointSlice{}\n\tfor _, sliceName := range sliceNamesToDelete.UnsortedList() {\n\t\tslicesToDelete = append(slicesToDelete, slicesByName[sliceName])\n\t}\n\n\treturn slicesToCreate, slicesToUpdate, slicesToDelete, numAdded, numRemoved\n}\n\nfunc (r *Reconciler) DeleteService(namespace, name string) {\n\tr.metricsCache.DeleteService(types.NamespacedName{Namespace: namespace, Name: name})\n}\n\nfunc (r *Reconciler) GetControllerName() string {\n\treturn r.controllerName\n}\n\n// ManagedByChanged returns true if one of the provided EndpointSlices is\n// managed by the != r.ManagedByController(endpointSlice2)\n}\n\n// ManagedByController returns true if the controller of the provided\n// EndpointSlices is the EndpointSlice controller.\nfunc (r *Reconciler) ManagedByController(endpointSlice *discovery.EndpointSlice) bool {\n\tmanagedBy := endpointSlice.Labels[discovery.LabelManagedBy]\n\treturn managedBy == r.controllerName\n}\n",

94\u2192\t// for further adjustment\n    95\u2192\tfor _, existingSlice := range existingSlices {\n    96\u2192\t\t// service no longer supports that address type, add it to deleted slices\n    97\u2192\t\tif !serviceSupportedAddressesTypes.Has(existingSlice.AddressType) {\n    98\u2192\t\t\tif r.topologyCache != nil {\n    99\u2192\t\t\t\tsvcKey, err := ServiceControllerKey(existingSlice)\n   100\u2192\t\t\t\tif err != nil {\n   101\u2192\t\t\t\t\tlogger.Info(\"Couldn't get key to remove EndpointSlice from topology cache\", \"existingSlice\", existingSlice, \"err\", err)\n   102\u2192\t\t\t\t} else {\n   103\u2192\t\t\t\t\tr.topologyCache.RemoveHints(svcKey, existingSlice.AddressType)\n   104\u2192\t\t\t\t}\n   105\u2192\t\t\t}\n   106\u2192\n   107\u2192\t\t\tslicesToDelete = append(slicesToDelete, existingSlice)\n   108\u2192\t\t\tcontinue\n   109\u2192\t\t}\n   110\u2192\n   111\u2192\t\t// add list if it is not on our map\n   112\u2192\t\tif _, ok := slicesByAddressType[existingSlice.AddressType]; !ok {\n   113\u2192\t\t\tslicesByAddressType[existingSlice.AddressType] = make([]*discovery.EndpointSlice, 0, 1)\n   114\u2192\t\t}\n   115\u2192\n   116\u2192\t\tslicesByAddressType[existingSlice.AddressType] = append(slicesByAddressType[existingSlice.AddressType], existingSlice)\n   117\u2192\t}\n   118\u2192\n   119\u2192\t// reconcile for existing.\n   120\u2192\tfor addressType := range serviceSupportedAddressesTypes {\n   121\u2192\t\texistingSlices := slicesByAddressType[addressType]\n   122\u2192\t\terr 126\u2192\t}\n   127\u2192\n   128\u2192\t// delete those which are of addressType that is no longer supported\n   129\u2192\t// by the service\n   130\u2192\tfor _, sliceToDelete := range 135\u2192\t\t\tr.endpointSliceTracker.ExpectDeletion(sliceToDelete)\n   136\u2192\t\t\tmetrics.EndpointSliceChanges.WithLabelValues(\"delete\").Inc()\n   137\u2192\t\t}\n   138\u2192\t}\n   139\u2192\n   140\u2192\treturn utilerrors.NewAggregate(errs)\n   141\u2192}\n   142\u2192\n   143\u2192// reconcileByAddressType takes a set of pods currently matching a service selector and\n   144\u2192// compares them with the endpoints already present in any existing endpoint\n   145\u2192// slices (by address type) for the given service. It creates, updates, or deletes endpoint slices\n   146\u2192// to ensure the desired set of pods are represented by endpoint slices.\n   147\u2192func (r *Reconciler) reconcileByAddressType(logger will remove the Pod, but we want to avoid\n   198\u2192\t\t\t// situations where a reference from a Pod to a missing node can leave the EndpointSlice\n   199\u2192\t\t\t// stuck forever.\n   200\u2192\t\t\t// On the other side, if the service.Spec.PublishNotReadyAddresses is set we just add the\n   201\u2192\t\t\t// Pod, since the user is explicitly indicating that the Pod address should service.Namespace, service.Name, pod.Spec.NodeName))\n   205\u2192\t\t\t\tcontinue\n   206\u2192\t\t\t}\n   207\u2192\t\t}\n   208\u2192\t\tendpoint := podToEndpoint(pod, node, service, addressType)\n 219\u2192\tfor portMap, desiredEndpoints := range desiredEndpointsByPortMap {\n   220\u2192\t\tnumEndpoints := len(desiredEndpoints)\n   221\u2192\t\tpmSlicesToCreate, pmSlicesToUpdate, 224\u2192\t\ttotalAdded += added\n   225\u2192\t\ttotalRemoved += removed\n   226\u2192\n   227\u2192\t\tspMetrics.Set(portMap, metrics.EfficiencyInfo{\n   228\u2192\t\t\tEndpoints: numEndpoints,\n   229\u2192\t\t\tSlices:    len(existingSlicesByPortMap[portMap]) + len(pmSlicesToCreate) - len(pmSlicesToDelete),\n   230\u2192\t\t})\n   231\u2192\n   232\u2192\t\tslicesToCreate = 246\u2192\tif len(existingSlices) == len(slicesToDelete) && len(slicesToCreate) < 1 {\n   247\u2192\t\t// Check for existing placeholder slice outside of the core control flow\n   248\u2192\t\tplaceholderSlice := newEndpointSlice(logger, service, &endpointMeta{ports: []discovery.EndpointPort{}, addressType: addressType}, r.controllerName)\n   249\u2192\t\tif len(slicesToDelete) == 1 && placeholderSliceCompare.DeepEqual(slicesToDelete[0], placeholderSlice) {\n   250\u2192\t\t\t// We are about to unnecessarily delete/recreate the placeholder, remove it now.\n   251\u2192\t\t\tslicesToDelete = slicesToDelete[:0]\n   252\u2192\t\t} else {\n   253\u2192\t\t\tslicesToCreate = append(slicesToCreate, placeholderSlice)\n   254\u2192\t\t}\n   255\u2192\t\tspMetrics.Set(endpointsliceutil.NewPortMapKey(placeholderSlice.Ports), metrics.EfficiencyInfo{\n   256\u2192\t\t\tEndpoints: 0,\n   257\u2192\t\t\tSlices:    1,\n   258\u2192\t\t})\n   259\u2192\t}\n   260\u2192\n   261\u2192\tmetrics.EndpointsAddedPerSync.WithLabelValues().Observe(float64(totalAdded))\n   262\u2192\tmetrics.EndpointsRemovedPerSync.WithLabelValues().Observe(float64(totalRemoved))\n   263\u2192\n   264\u2192\tserviceNN := types.NamespacedName{Name: service.Name, Namespace: service.Namespace}\n   265\u2192\tr.metricsCache.UpdateServicePortCache(serviceNN, spMetrics)\n   266\u2192\n   267\u2192\t// Topology hints are assigned per address type. This means it is\n   268\u2192\t// theoretically possible for endpoints of one address type to be assigned\n   269\u2192\t// hints while another endpoints of another address type are not.\n   270\u2192\tsi := &topologycache.SliceInfo{\n   271\u2192\t\tServiceKey:  fmt.Sprintf(\"%s/%s\", service.Namespace, service.Name),\n   272\u2192\t\tAddressType: addressType,\n   273\u2192\t\tToCreate:    slicesToCreate,\n   274\u2192\t\tToUpdate:    slicesToUpdate,\n   275\u2192\t\tUnchanged:   unchangedSlices(existingSlices, slicesToUpdate, slicesToDelete),\n   276\u2192\t}\n   277\u2192\n   278\u2192\tcanUseTrafficDistribution := r.trafficDistributionEnabled && !hintsEnabled(service.Annotations)\n   279\u2192\n   280\u2192\t// Check if we need to add/remove hints based on the topology annotation.\n   281\u2192\t//\n   282\u2192\t// This if/else clause can be removed once the annotation has been deprecated.\n   283\u2192\t// Ref: https://github.com/kubernetes/enhancements/tree/master/keps/sig-network/4444-service-routing-preference\n   284\u2192\tif r.topologyCache != nil && hintsEnabled(service.Annotations) {\n   285\u2192\t\t// Reaching this point means that we need to configure hints based on the\n   286\u2192\t\t// topology annotation.\n   287\u2192\t\tslicesToCreate, slicesToUpdate, events = r.topologyCache.AddHints(logger, si)\n   288\u2192\n   289\u2192\t} else {\n   290\u2192\t\t// Reaching this point means that we will not be configuring hints based on\n   291\u2192\t\t// the topology annotation. We need to do 2 things:\n   292\u2192\t\t//  1. If hints were added previously based on the annotation, we need to\n   293\u2192\t\t//     clear up any locally cached hints from the topologyCache object.\n   294\u2192\t\t//  2. In other\n   296\u2192\t\t//     words, if we know that the `trafficDistribution` field has been\n   297\u2192\t\t//     correctly configured by the customer, we DO NOT remove the hints and\n   298\u2192\t\t//     wait for the trafficDist handlers to correctly configure them. Always\n   299\u2192\t\t//     unconditionally removing hints here (and letting them get readded by\n   300\u2192\t\t//     the trafficDist) adds extra overhead in the form of DeepCopy (done\n   301\u2192\t\t//     within topologyCache.RemoveHints)\n   302\u2192\n   303\u2192\t\t// Check 1.\n   304\u2192\t\tif r.topologyCache != nil {\n   305\u2192\t\t\tif 326\u2192\t\tr.metricsCache.UpdateTrafficDistributionForService(serviceNN, nil)\n   327\u2192\t}\n   328\u2192\n   329\u2192\terr := r.finalize(service, slicesToCreate, slicesToUpdate, slicesToDelete, triggerTime)\n   330\u2192\tif err != nil {\n   331\u2192\t\terrs = append(errs, err)\n   332\u2192\t}\n   333\u2192\tfor _, event := range events {\n   334\u2192\t\tr.eventRecorder.Event(service, event.EventType, event.Reason, event.Message)\n   335\u2192\t}\n   336\u2192\treturn utilerrors.NewAggregate(errs)\n   337\u2192\n   338\u2192}\n   339\u2192\n   340\u2192func NewReconciler(client clientset.Interface, nodeLister corelisters.NodeLister, maxEndpointsPerSlice int32, endpointSliceTracker *endpointsliceutil.EndpointSliceTracker, topologyCache *topologycache.TopologyCache, eventRecorder record.EventRecorder, controllerName string, options ...ReconcilerOption) *Reconciler {\n   341\u2192\tr := &Reconciler{\n   342\u2192\t\tclient:               client,\n   343\u2192\t\tnodeLister:           nodeLister,\n   344\u2192\t\tmaxEndpointsPerSlice: maxEndpointsPerSlice,\n   345\u2192\t\tendpointSliceTracker: endpointSliceTracker,\n   346\u2192\t\tmetricsCache:         metrics.NewCache(maxEndpointsPerSlice),\n   347\u2192\t\ttopologyCache:        topologyCache,\n   348\u2192\t\teventRecorder:        eventRecorder,\n   349\u2192\t\tcontrollerName:       controllerName,\n   350\u2192\t}\n   351\u2192\tfor _, option := range options {\n   352\u2192\t\toption(r)\n   353\u2192\t}\n   354\u2192\treturn r\n   355\u2192}\n   356\u2192\n   357\u2192// placeholderSliceCompare is a conversion func for comparing two placeholder endpoint slices.\n   358\u2192// It only compares the specific fields we care about.\n   359\u2192var placeholderSliceCompare = conversion.EqualitiesOrDie(\n   360\u2192\tfunc(a, b metav1.OwnerReference) bool {\n   361\u2192\t\treturn a.String() == b.String()\n   362\u2192\t},\n   363\u2192\tfunc(a, b metav1.ObjectMeta) bool {\n   364\u2192\t\tif a.Namespace != b.Namespace {\n   365\u2192\t\t\treturn false\n   366\u2192\t\t}\n   367\u2192\t\tfor k, v := range a.Labels {\n   368\u2192\t\t\tif b.Labels[k] != v {\n   369\u2192\t\t\t\treturn false\n   370\u2192\t\t\t}\n   371\u2192\t\t}\n   372\u2192\t\tfor k, v := range b.Labels {\n   373\u2192\t\t\tif a.Labels[k] != v {\n   374\u2192\t\t\t\treturn false\n   375\u2192\t\t\t}\n   376\u2192\t\t}\n   377\u2192\t\treturn true\n   378\u2192\t},\n   379\u2192)\n   380\u2192\n   381\u2192// finalize creates, updates, and deletes slices as specified\n   382\u2192func (r *Reconciler) finalize(\n   383\u2192\tservice *corev1.Service,\n   384\u2192\tslicesToCreate,\n   385\u2192\tslicesToUpdate,\n   386\u2192\tslicesToDelete []*discovery.EndpointSlice,\n   387\u2192\ttriggerTime time.Time,\n   388\u2192) error {\n   389\u2192\t// If there are slices to create and delete, change the creates to updates\n   390\u2192\t// of the slices that would otherwise be deleted.\n   391\u2192\tfor i := 0; i < len(slicesToDelete); {\n   392\u2192\t\tif len(slicesToCreate) == 0 {\n   393\u2192\t\t\tbreak\n   394\u2192\t\t}\n   395\u2192\t\tsliceToDelete := slicesToDelete[i]\n   396\u2192\t\tslice := slicesToCreate[len(slicesToCreate)-1]\n   397\u2192\t\t// Only update EndpointSlices that are owned by this Service and have\n   398\u2192\t\t// the same AddressType. We need to avoid updating EndpointSlices that\n   399\u2192\t\t// are being garbage collected for an old Service with the same name.\n   400\u2192\t\t// The AddressType field is immutable. Since Services also consider\n   401\u2192\t\t// IPFamily immutable, the only case where this should matter will be\n   402\u2192\t\t// the migration from IP to IPv4 and IPv6 AddressTypes, where there's a\n   403\u2192\t\t// chance EndpointSlices with an IP AddressType would otherwise be\n   404\u2192\t\t// updated to IPv4 or IPv6 without this check.\n   405\u2192\t\tif sliceToDelete.AddressType == slice.AddressType && ownedBy(sliceToDelete, service) {\n   406\u2192\t\t\tslice.Name = sliceToDelete.Name\n   407\u2192\t\t\tslicesToCreate = slicesToCreate[:len(slicesToCreate)-1]\n   408\u2192\t\t\tslicesToUpdate = append(slicesToUpdate, slice)\n   409\u2192\t\t\tslicesToDelete = append(slicesToDelete[:i], slicesToDelete[i+1:]...)\n   410\u2192\t\t} else {\n   411\u2192\t\t\ti++\n   412\u2192\t\t}\n   413\u2192\t}\n   414\u2192\n   415\u2192\t// Don't create new EndpointSlices if the Service is pending deletion. This\n   416\u2192\t// is to avoid a potential race condition with the garbage collector where\n   417\u2192\t// it tries to delete EndpointSlices as this controller replaces them.\n   418\u2192\tif service.DeletionTimestamp == nil {\n   419\u2192\t\tfor _, endpointSlice := range slicesToCreate {\n   420\u2192\t\t\taddTriggerTimeAnnotation(endpointSlice, triggerTime)\n   421\u2192\t\t\tcreatedSlice, err := r.client.DiscoveryV1().EndpointSlices(service.Namespace).Create(context.TODO(), endpointSlice, metav1.CreateOptions{})\n   422\u2192\t\t\tif err != nil {\n   423\u2192\t\t\t\t// If the namespace is terminating, creates will continue to fail. Simply drop the item.\n   424\u2192\t\t\t\tif errors.HasStatusCause(err, corev1.NamespaceTerminatingCause) {\n   425\u2192\t\t\t\t\treturn nil\n   426\u2192\t\t\t\t}\n   427\u2192\t\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"failed to create EndpointSlice for Service %s/%s: %v\", service.Namespace, service.Name, err)\n   428\u2192\t\t\t}\n   429\u2192\t\t\tr.endpointSliceTracker.Update(createdSlice)\n   430\u2192\t\t\tmetrics.EndpointSliceChanges.WithLabelValues(\"create\").Inc()\n   431\u2192\t\t}\n   432\u2192\t}\n   433\u2192\n   434\u2192\tfor _, endpointSlice := range slicesToUpdate {\n   435\u2192\t\taddTriggerTimeAnnotation(endpointSlice, triggerTime)\n   436\u2192\t\tupdatedSlice, err := r.client.DiscoveryV1().EndpointSlices(service.Namespace).Update(context.TODO(), endpointSlice, metav1.UpdateOptions{})\n   437\u2192\t\tif err != nil {\n   438\u2192\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"failed to update %s EndpointSlice for Service %s/%s: %v\", endpointSlice.Name, service.Namespace, service.Name, err)\n   439\u2192\t\t}\n   440\u2192\t\tr.endpointSliceTracker.Update(updatedSlice)\n   441\u2192\t\tmetrics.EndpointSliceChanges.WithLabelValues(\"update\").Inc()\n   442\u2192\t}\n   443\u2192\n   444\u2192\tfor _, endpointSlice := range slicesToDelete {\n   445\u2192\t\terr := r.client.DiscoveryV1().EndpointSlices(service.Namespace).Delete(context.TODO(), endpointSlice.Name, metav1.DeleteOptions{})\n   446\u2192\t\tif err != nil {\n   447\u2192\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"failed to delete %s EndpointSlice for Service %s/%s: %v\", endpointSlice.Name, service.Namespace, 469\u2192\n   470\u2192// reconcileByPortMapping compares the endpoints found in existing slices with\n   471\u2192// the list of desired endpoints and returns lists of slices to create, update,\n   472\u2192// and delete. It also checks that the slices mirror the parent services labels.\n   473\u2192// The logic is split up into several main steps:\n   474\u2192//  1. It also checks\n   476\u2192//     if the slices have the labels of the parent services, and updates them if not.\n   477\u2192//  2. 593\u2192\t\t\tsliceToFill = sliceToFill.DeepCopy()\n   594\u2192\t\t\tslicesByName[sliceToFill.Name] = sliceToFill\n   595\u2192\t\t}\n   596\u2192\n   597\u2192\t\t// Fill the slice up with Kubernetes controller framework pattern that differs from controller-runtime. Here's how it works:\\n\\n## Controller Registration Pattern\\n\\n### 1. Reconciler Interface Definition\\nThe Reconciler concept is implemented as controller structs like `DeploymentController` (kubernetes/kubernetes:pkg/controller/deployment/deployment_controller.go:66-98). The struct contains:\\n- Kubernetes clients and listers from k8s.io/client-go\\n- A work queue (workqueue.TypedRateLimitingInterface) for items to reconcile\\n- Event recorder for publishing events\\n- A syncHandler function that implements the reconciliation logic\\n\\n### 2. SetupWithManager Equivalent\\nInstead of SetupWithManager(), Kubernetes uses a two-step initialization pattern:\\n\\n**Step 1: Controller Instantiation** (kubernetes/kubernetes:pkg/controller/deployment/deployment_controller.go:100-159)\\n- NewDeploymentController() factory function creates the controller instance\\n- Registers informer event handlers (AddEventHandler) for Deployments, ReplicaSets, and Pods\\n- Each handler (AddFunc, UpdateFunc, DeleteFunc) enqueues items for reconciliation\\n- Stores informer listers and synced signals for dependency tracking\\n\\n**Step 2: Manager Integration** (kubernetes/kubernetes:cmd/kube-controller-manager/app/apps.go:106-119)\\n- startDeploymentController() function instantiates the controller\\n- Calls dc.Run(ctx, workers) to start the reconciliation loop\\n- The manager passes a ControllerContext containing InformerFactory, ClientBuilder, and ComponentConfig\\n\\n### 3. Manager's Reconcile Loop Wiring\\nThe wiring happens in the controller manager:\\n\\n**ControllerContext** (kubernetes/kubernetes:cmd/kube-controller-manager/app/controllermanager.go:366-401) serves as the manager equivalent, providing:\\n- ClientBuilder for Kubernetes API clients\\n- InformerFactory for creating Informers and Listers\\n- ObjectOrMetadataInformerFactory for generic resource handling\\n- InformersStarted signal for synchronization\\n\\n**Control Flow Chain**:\\n1. Run() function (kubernetes/kubernetes:cmd/kube-controller-manager/app/controllermanager.go:175) creates ControllerContext via CreateControllerContext()\\n2. StartControllers() (kubernetes/kubernetes:cmd/kube-controller-manager/app/controllermanager.go) iterates through controller descriptors and calls their initFunc\\n3. Each controller's initFunc (e.g., startDeploymentController) instantiates the controller and calls Run()\\n4. InformerFactory.Start() begins syncing informers\\n5. Controllers process work queue items in a worker loop (kubernetes/kubernetes:pkg/controller/deployment/deployment_controller.go:162-185)\\n\\n### 4. Reconciliation Loop Implementation\\nThe Run() method implements the reconciliation loop:\\n- Waits for informer caches to sync using WaitForNamedCacheSync()\\n- Spawns worker goroutines that call wait.UntilWithContext()\\n- Each worker continuously calls the syncHandler function for queued items\\n- The syncHandler (syncDeployment) compares current vs desired state and updates accordingly\\n\\n## Example: EndpointSlice Reconciler\\nThe k8s.io/endpointslice module (kubernetes/kubernetes:staging/src/k8s.io/endpointslice/reconciler.go) provides another reconciliation pattern used within controllers. The Reconciler struct (lines 45-60) and NewReconciler() factory (lines 340-355) show:\\n- Configuration via ReconcilerOption pattern (line 62)\\n- Reconciliation method: Reconcile() (line 83) that transforms EndpointSlice state\\n- Finalization logic that creates, updates, or deletes endpoint slices\\n\\n## Key Differences from controller-runtime\\nKubernetes implements its own mature controller framework that:\\n- Uses explicit informers and listers instead of abstractions\\n- Manages work queues directly\\n- Doesn't use a Manager abstraction for registration (uses ControllerContext instead)\\n- Controllers manage their own event handler registration\\n- Uses context.Context throughout for lifecycle management\\n- Implements exponential backoff rate limiting via workqueue\"\n}\n",
